25/02/25, 3:51â€¯pm - Suyash baby: #include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;

class ds {
private:
    unordered_map<int, int> valueCountMap; 
    unordered_map<int, vector<int>> valuePositionMap; 
    vector<int> values; 
    int minValue;
    int minPosition; 
   
public:
    ds() {
        srand(time(0));
        minValue = INT_MAX;
        minPosition = -1;
    }
   
  
    bool insert(int val) {
        bool isNew = false;
       
       
        if (valueCountMap.find(val) == valueCountMap.end() || valueCountMap[val] == 0) {
            isNew = true;
        }
       
       
        valueCountMap[val]++;
        valuePositionMap[val].push_back(values.size());
        values.push_back(val);
       
       
        if (isNew) {
            if (val < minValue) {
                minValue = val;
                minPosition = values.size() - 1;
            }
        }
       
        return isNew;
    }
   
   
    bool remove(int val) {
        if (valueCountMap.find(val) == valueCountMap.end() || valueCountMap[val] == 0) {
            return false; 
        }
       
       
        valueCountMap[val]--;
       
       
        valuePositionMap[val].pop_back();
       
       
        if (valueCountMap[val] == 0) {
            valuePositionMap.erase(val);
        }
       
        
        if (valueCountMap[val] == 0) {
          
            minValue = INT_MAX;
            minPosition = -1;
            for (int i = 0; i < values.size(); ++i) {
                if (valueCountMap[values[i]] > 0 && values[i] < minValue) {
                    minValue = values[i];
                    minPosition = i;
                }
            }
        }
       
        return true;
    }
   
   
    int getRandom() {
        int totalElements = 0;
       
        
        for (const auto& entry : valueCountMap) {
            totalElements += entry.second;
        }
       
  
        int randomIndex = rand() % totalElements;
       
        
        int count = 0;
        for (const auto& entry : valueCountMap) {
            count += entry.second;
            if (randomIndex < count) {
                return entry.first;
            }
        }
       
        return -1; 
    }
   
   
    pair<int, int> getMin() {
        return {minValue, minPosition};
    }
};


int main() {
    ds mySet;
   
    mySet.insert(3);
    mySet.insert(1);
    mySet.insert(5);
    mySet.insert(3);
   
    cout << "Random element: " << mySet.getRandom() << endl;
    pair<int, int> minElement = mySet.getMin();
    cout << "Minimum element: " << minElement.first << " at position " << minElement.second << endl;
   
    mySet.remove(3);
   
    cout << "Random element after removal: " << mySet.getRandom() << endl;
    minElement = mySet.getMin();
    cout << "Minimum element after removal: " << minElement.first << " at position " << minElement.second << endl;
   
    return 0;
}
25/02/25, 3:53â€¯pm - Suryanshu: #include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>

int main() {
    int arr[100] = {1, 2, 3, 4, 5};
    int n = 5, value = 3;  // Try inserting value 3 (which is already present)

    // Check if the value is already present
    int found = 0;
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        if (arr[i] == value) {
            // If present, delete it by shifting elements to the left
            for (int j = i; j < n - 1; j++) {
                arr[j] = arr[j + 1];
            }
            n--;  // Decrease the array size
            found = 1;
            printf("Element %d deleted.\n", value);
            break;
        }
    }

    // If the value was not found, add it to the end
    if (!found) {
        arr[n++] = value;
        printf("Element %d added.\n", value);
    }

    // Randomly access an element
    int randomIndex = rand() % n;
    printf("Randomly accessed element: %d\n", arr[randomIndex]);

    // Find the minimum element and its position
    int min = arr[0], minPos = 0;
    for (int i = 1; i < n; i++) {
        if (arr[i] < min) {
            min = arr[i];
            minPos = i;
        }
    }

    // Output minimum element and its position
    printf("Minimum element: %d, Position: %d\n", min, minPos);

    return 0;
}
